365→\n   366→// RemovePodFinalizers removes pod finalizers for the pods\n   367→func RemovePodFinalizers(ctx context.Context, cs clientset.Interface, t *testing.T, pods ...v1.Pod) {\n   368→\tt.Helper()\n   369→\tfor _, p := range pods {\n   370→\t\tpod, err := cs.CoreV1().Pods(p.Namespace).Get(ctx, p.Name, metav1.GetOptions{})\n   371→\t\tif err != nil && !apierrors.IsNotFound(err) 384→\t\t\t}\n   385→\t\t}\n   386→\t}\n   387→}\n   388→\n   389→// CleanupPods deletes the given pods and waits for them to be actually deleted.\n   390→func CleanupPods(ctx context.Context, cs []v1.Taint) wait.ConditionWithContextFunc {\n   442→\treturn func(context.Context) (bool, error) {\n   443→\t\tnode, err := cs.CoreV1().Nodes().Get(ctx, nodeName, metav1.GetOptions{})\n   444→\t\tif err != nil {\n   445→\t\t\treturn false, err\n   446→\t\t}\n   447→\n   448→\t\t// node.Spec.Taints may have more taints\n   449→\t\tif len(taints) > len(node.Spec.Taints) {\n   450→\t\t\treturn v1.NodeReady {\n   468→\t\t\tcontinue\n   469→\t\t}\n   470→\t\t// Just return the first condition with type NodeReady\n   471→\t\treturn c.Status, nil\n   472→\t}\n   473→\treturn v1.ConditionFalse, errors.New(\"None of the conditions is of type NodeReady\")\n   474→}\n   475→\n   476→// GetTolerationSeconds gets the period of time the toleration\n   477→func GetTolerationSeconds(tolerations see is in the store. Used to observe reflected events.\n   740→func WaitForReflection(ctx context.Context, t *testing.T, nodeLister corelisters.NodeLister, key string,\n   741→\tpassFunc func(n interface{}) bool) error {\n   742→\tvar nodes []*v1.Node\n   743→\terr := wait.PollUntilContextTimeout(ctx, time.Millisecond*100, wait.ForeverTestTimeout, false, func(context.Context) (bool, error) {\n   744→\t\tn, err := nodeLister.Get(key)\n   745→\n   746→\t\tswitch {\n   747→\t\tcase err == nil && passFunc(n):\n   748→\t\t\treturn true, nil\n   749→\t\tcase apierrors.IsNotFound(err):\n   750→\t\t\tnodes = append(nodes, nil)\n   751→\t\tcase err != nil:\n   752→\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"Unexpected error: %v\", err)\n   753→\t\tdefault:\n   754→\t\t\tnodes = append(nodes, n)\n   755→\t\t}\n   756→\n   757→\t\treturn false, nil\n   758→\t})\n   759→\tif err != nil {\n   760→\t\tt.Logf(\"Logging consecutive node versions received from store:\")\n   761→\t\tfor i, n := range nodes {\n   762→\t\t\tt.Logf(\"%d: %#v\", i, n)\n   763→\t\t}\n   764→\t}\n   765→\treturn err\n   766→}\n   767→\n   768→func UpdateNode(cs clientset.Interface, node *v1.Node) (*v1.Node, error) {\n   769→\treturn cs.CoreV1().Nodes().Update(context.TODO(), node, metav1.UpdateOptions{})\n   770→}\n   771→\n   772→func CreateNode(cs clientset.Interface, node *v1.Node) (*v1.Node, error) {\n 1004→func PodScheduledIn(c clientset.Interface, podNamespace, podName string, nodeNames []string) wait.ConditionWithContextFunc {\n  1005→\treturn func(ctx context.Context) (bool, error) {\n CreateNamespacesWithLabels(cs clientset.Interface, namespaces []string, labels map[string]string) error {\n  1150→\tfor _, n := range namespaces {\n  1151→\t\tns := v1.Namespace{ObjectMeta:  1155→\t}\n  1156→\treturn nil\n  1157→}\n  1158→\n  1159→// timeout returns a timeout error if the given `f` function doesn't\n  1160→// complete within `d` duration; otherwise it returns nil.\n  1161→func timeout(ctx context.Context, d time.Duration, f func()) error {\n  1162→\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(ctx, d)\n  1163→\tdefer cancel()\n  1164→\n  1165→\tdone := make(chan struct{})\n  1166→\tgo func() {\n  1167→\t\tf()\n  1168→\t\tclose(done)\n  1169→\t}()\n  1170→\n  1171→\tselect {\n  1172→\tcase <-done:\n  1173→\t\treturn nil\n  1174→\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n  1175→\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n  1176→\t}\n  1177→}\n  1178→\n  1179→// NextPodOrDie returns the next Pod in the scheduler queue.\n  1180→// The operation needs to be completed within 5 seconds; otherwise the test gets metav1.GetOptions{})\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn false, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// node.Spec.Taints may have more taints\n\t\tif len(taints) > len(node.Spec.Taints) {\n\t\t\treturn false, NodeReadyStatus returns the status of first condition with type NodeReady.\n// If none of the condition is of type NodeReady, returns an error.\nfunc NodeReadyStatus(conditions []v1.NodeCondition) WaitForReflection waits till the passFunc confirms that the object it expects\n// to see is in the store. Used to observe reflected events.\nfunc WaitForReflection(ctx context.Context, t *testing.T, nodeLister corelisters.NodeLister, key string,\n\tpassFunc func(n interface{}) bool) error {\n\tvar nodes []*v1.Node\n\terr := wait.PollUntilContextTimeout(ctx, time.Millisecond*100, wait.ForeverTestTimeout, false, func(context.Context) (bool, error) {\n\t\tn, err := nodeLister.Get(key)\n\n\t\tswitch {\n\t\tcase err == nil && passFunc(n):\n\t\t\treturn true, nil\n\t\tcase apierrors.IsNotFound(err):\n\t\t\tnodes = append(nodes, nil)\n\t\tcase err != nil:\n\t\t\tt.Errorf(\"Unexpected error: %v\", err)\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tnodes = append(nodes, n)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn false, nil\n\t})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Logf(\"Logging consecutive node versions received from store:\")\n\t\tfor i, n := range nodes {\n\t\t\tt.Logf(\"%d: %#v\", i, n)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn err\n}\n\nfunc UpdateNode(cs clientset.Interface, node *v1.Node) (*v1.Node, error) {\n\treturn onto one of the expected nodes.\nfunc PodScheduledIn(c clientset.Interface, podNamespace, podName string, nodeNames []string) wait.ConditionWithContextFunc {\n\treturn func(ctx context.Context) (bool, error) {\n\t\tpod, err := c.CoreV1().Pods(podNamespace).Get(ctx, podName, metav1.GetOptions{})\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t// This could be a connection error so we want to retry.\n\t\t\treturn false, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tif pod.Spec.NodeName == \"\" {\n\t\t\treturn false, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor _, nodeName := range nodeNames {\n\t\t\tif pod.Spec.NodeName == nodeName {\n\t\t\t\treturn true, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn false, nil\n\t}\n}\n\n// PodUnschedulable returns a condition function that returns true if the given pod\n// gets unschedulable status of reason 'Unschedulable'.\nfunc PodUnschedulable(c clientset.Interface, podNamespace, podName string) wait.ConditionWithContextFunc {\n\treturn func(ctx context.Context) (bool, error) {\n\t\tpod, err := c.CoreV1().Pods(podNamespace).Get(ctx, podName, metav1.GetOptions{})\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t// This could be a connection error so we want to retry.\n\t\t\treturn false, nil\n\t\t}\n\t\t_, cond := podutil.GetPodCondition(&pod.Status, v1.PodScheduled)\n\t\treturn cond != nil && cond.Status == v1.ConditionFalse &&\n\t\t\tcond.Reason == v1.PodReasonUnschedulable && pod.Spec.NodeName == \"\", nil\n\t}\n}\n\n// PodSchedulingError returns a condition function that returns true if the given pod\n// gets unschedulable status for reasons other than \"Unschedulable\". The scheduler\n// records such reasons in case of error.\nfunc PodSchedulingError(c clientset.Interface, podNamespace, podName string) wait.ConditionWithContextFunc {\n\treturn func(ctx
